b'After the successful conduct of \xe2\x80\x9c\xf0\x9d\x90\x8e\xf0\x9d\x90\xa9\xf0\x9d\x90\x9e\xf0\x9d\x90\xab\xf0\x9d\x90\x9a\xf0\x9d\x90\xad\xf0\x9d\x90\xa2\xf0\x9d\x90\xa8\xf0\x9d\x90\xa7 \xf0\x9d\x90\x81\xf0\x9d\x90\x9a\xf0\x9d\x90\xa4\xf0\x9d\x90\xa5\xf0\x9d\x90\x9a\xf0\x9d\x90\xac\xe2\x80\x9d in the vicinity of J.P Rizal St, Laoag City, representatives of Globe Telecommunications and PLDT paid a courtesy visit and dialogue with your Acting General Manager Cipriano \xe2\x80\x9cPerry\xe2\x80\x9d E. Martinez III to resolve and sort out concerns regarding the installation of their lines on INEC owned poles.  \n\nTo avoid the re-occurrence of unorganized and knotted dangling lines on INEC poles, your AGM required Globe and PLDT to secure the assistance of INEC before installing any of their lines on our poles. Otherwise, INEC will be compelled to cut and remove such lines. This is to ensure the structural integrity and non-obstruction of our poles and lines. \n\nThis afternoon, with INEC\xe2\x80\x99s permission and supervision, Globe Telecommunications started the restoration of their lines. PLDT is scheduled to re-install its lines tomorrow morning with the assistance of your INEC Team. \n\n- \xf0\x9d\x91\xaa\xf0\x9d\x92\x8a\xf0\x9d\x92\x91\xf0\x9d\x92\x93\xf0\x9d\x92\x8a\xf0\x9d\x92\x82\xf0\x9d\x92\x8f\xf0\x9d\x92\x90 \xe2\x80\x9c\xf0\x9d\x91\xb7\xf0\x9d\x92\x86\xf0\x9d\x92\x93\xf0\x9d\x92\x93\xf0\x9d\x92\x9a\xe2\x80\x9d \xf0\x9d\x91\xac. \xf0\x9d\x91\xb4\xf0\x9d\x92\x82\xf0\x9d\x92\x93\xf0\x9d\x92\x95\xf0\x9d\x92\x8a\xf0\x9d\x92\x8f\xf0\x9d\x92\x86\xf0\x9d\x92\x9b \xf0\x9d\x91\xb0\xf0\x9d\x91\xb0\xf0\x9d\x91\xb0,\n\xf0\x9d\x90\xbc\xf0\x9d\x91\x81\xf0\x9d\x90\xb8\xf0\x9d\x90\xb6 \xf0\x9d\x90\xb4\xf0\x9d\x91\x90\xf0\x9d\x91\xa1\xf0\x9d\x91\x96\xf0\x9d\x91\x9b\xf0\x9d\x91\x94 \xf0\x9d\x90\xba\xf0\x9d\x91\x92\xf0\x9d\x91\x9b\xf0\x9d\x91\x92\xf0\x9d\x91\x9f\xf0\x9d\x91\x8e\xf0\x9d\x91\x99 \xf0\x9d\x91\x80\xf0\x9d\x91\x8e\xf0\x9d\x91\x9b\xf0\x9d\x91\x8e\xf0\x9d\x91\x94\xf0\x9d\x91\x92\xf0\x9d\x91\x9f\n\n#INECofficial \n#INEC'
b'\xf0\x9d\x90\x86\xf0\x9d\x90\x8c\xe2\x80\x99\xf0\x9d\x90\xac \xf0\x9d\x90\x91\xf0\x9d\x90\x84\xf0\x9d\x90\x8f\xf0\x9d\x90\x8e\xf0\x9d\x90\x91\xf0\x9d\x90\x93 \nFebruary 19, 2024\n\nWe at INEC have been persistent in requiring telecommunication and cable companies to coordinate with your electric cooperative to organize the installed lines on our poles. However, to no avail and even after three months, telecommunication and cable companies refuse to cooperate and accede to this initiative of INEC. \n\nBecause of which, in the morning of 19 February 2024, the Ilocos Norte Electric Cooperative, Inc. headed by your Acting General Manager Cipriano \xe2\x80\x9cPerry\xe2\x80\x9d E. b'INEC PRESS RELEASE\n\nOn 14 February 2024, the Electrician Workers Guild of Ilocos Norte (EWGIN) visited the office of your Acting General Manager, Cipriano \xe2\x80\x9cPerry\xe2\x80\x9d E. Martinez III for a courtesy call and discuss matters that will strengthen the relationship between your electric cooperatove and their association. \n\nAmong other matters, INEC and EWGIN discussed ways to move forward to solidify their partnership towards lessening the cases of illegal tapping and pilferage in the province. \n\nIt is to be noted that pilferage converts to systems losses that are passed on to the member-consumer-owners in your monthly billing. For February 2024, the systems loss amounts to P0.7262 per kwH. \n\nHowever, we remain our steadfast commitment of reducing the systems losses in the province as a part of our resolution to the continuous decrease of electricity rates in the Province of Ilocos Norte.\n\n#INECofficial \n#INEC \n#INECpressrelease'

b'\xf0\x9d\x90\x86\xf0\x9d\x90\x8c\xe2\x80\x99\xf0\x9d\x90\xac \xf0\x9d\x90\x91\xf0\x9d\x90\x84\xf0\x9d\x90\x8f\xf0\x9d\x90\x8e\xf0\x9d\x90\x91\xf0\x9d\x90\x93 \nFebruary 8, 2023 \n\nThe Ilocos Norte Electric Cooperative, Inc. (INEC) presents a three month comparative report of our electricity rates from December 2023 to February 2024. \n\nPlease take note of the uniqueness of the January 2024 rates. The ERC in a December order mandated INEC to deduct and make a one time refund of \xe2\x80\x9cover-recovery\xe2\x80\x9d the amount of which P1.6195 was deducted from the computed generation charge of P6. 2163 which resulted in INEC collecting the much reduced rate of P4.5968 as Generation Charge per kw/h.  Hence, the monthly rate of P8.8637 for January. \n\nThe further decline in the electricity costs can be attributed primarily to the efficient trading on the energy market of our INEC trading team. This is highlighted in the continuing monthly decline of the generation charges from P6.5023 (December 2023) to P6.2779 (February 2024) totaling to P0.2244 decrease in generation charge in a span of three months. \n\nIndeed, the electricity cost in  the Province of Ilocos Norte has undergone a total of P4.1601 decrease in a span of 5 month from the August 2023 to February 2024\n\nWe at your INEC, reiterate our commitment in sustaining our efforts in lowering our electricity rates. We assure you that we remain steadfast in our commitment in finding ways to reduce electricity costs in the Province of Ilocos Norte. \n\n-\xf0\x9d\x91\xaa\xf0\x9d\x92\x8a\xf0\x9d\x92\x91\xf0\x9d\x92\x93\xf0\x9d\x92\x8a\xf0\x9d\x92\x82\xf0\x9d\x92\x8f\xf0\x9d\x92\x90 \xe2\x80\x9c\xf0\x9d\x91\xb7\xf0\x9d\x92\x86\xf0\x9d\x92\x93\xf0\x9d\x92\x93\xf0\x9d\x92\x9a\xe2\x80\x9d \xf0\x9d\x91\xac. \xf0\x9d\x91\xb4\xf0\x9d\x92\x82\xf0\x9d\x92\x93\xf0\x9d\x92\x95\xf0\x9d\x92\x8a\xf0\x9d\x92\x8f\xf0\x9d\x92\x86\xf0\x9d\x92\x9b \xf0\x9d\x91\xb0\xf0\x9d\x91\xb0\xf0\x9d\x91\xb0,\n\xf0\x9d\x90\xbc\xf0\x9d\x91\x81\xf0\x9d\x90\xb8\xf0\x9d\x90\xb6 \xf0\x9d\x90\xb4\xf0\x9d\x91\x90\xf0\x9d\x91\xa1\xf0\x9d\x91\x96\xf0\x9d\x91\x9b\xf0\x9d\x91\x94 \xf0\x9d\x90\xba\xf0\x9d\x91\x92\xf0\x9d\x91\x9b\xf0\x9d\x91\x92\xf0\x9d\x91\x9f\xf0\x9d\x91\x8e\xf0\x9d\x91\x99 \xf0\x9d\x91\x80\xf0\x9d\x91\x8e\xf0\x9d\x91\x9b\xf0\x9d\x91\x8e\xf0\x9d\x91\x94\xf0\x9d\x91\x92\xf0\x9d\x91\x9f\n\n#INECofficial \n#INEC \n#INECrates\n#INECgmreport'

b'\xf0\x9d\x90\x88\xf0\x9d\x90\x8d\xf0\x9d\x90\x84\xf0\x9d\x90\x82 \xf0\x9d\x90\x8f\xf0\x9d\x90\x91\xf0\x9d\x90\x84\xf0\x9d\x90\x92\xf0\x9d\x90\x92 \xf0\x9d\x90\x91\xf0\x9d\x90\x84\xf0\x9d\x90\x8b\xf0\x9d\x90\x84\xf0\x9d\x90\x80\xf0\x9d\x90\x92\xf0\x9d\x90\x84\nJanuary 20, 2024\n\nFor the past week, INEC management has been closely guarding the operations of the Laoag City Carnival. \n\nIt has come to our attention that illegal electric connections had been tapped on meters and submeters located at the area of the carnival. Upon checking the area and upon investigation, such connections were made without securing approval from INEC nor securing the necessary permits from the Bureau of Fire Protection. \n\nOn a daily basis, your AGM dispatch the area manager and linemen on duty to ensure that such illegal connections are removed at the Laoag City Fiesta Carnaval. However, such as the case this evening, illegal connections are repeatedly being put up and connected causing the probability of electrical overloading  to the detriment of the whole carnival and the general public. \n\nINEC has coordinated with Bureau of Fire Protection (BFP) Provincial Office and the Ilocos Norte Provincial Police Office (INPPO) to inspect and cause for the apprehension of any individual found to have made or cause to be made the illegal connections. \n\nWe warn the public that under RA 7832 or the "Anti-electricity and Electric Transmission Lines/Materials Pilferage Act of 1994,\xe2\x80\x9d tapping, making or causing to be made any connection to the existing electric service facilities without the electric utility\xe2\x80\x99s consent or authority is a form of ILLEGAL USE OF ELECTRICITY which is punishable by IMPRISONMENT OF SIX YEARS AND ONE DAY TO TWELVE YEARS and/or a FINE ranging from P10,000 to P20,000. \n\nWe ask for the cooperation of the operators and/or management of the Laoag City Fiesta Carnival to please prioritize the safety, security and welfare of the public above any financial gain and ensure that all electrical connections in the area are inspected and approved to be safe and secured by INEC and BFP. \n- \xf0\x9d\x91\xaa\xf0\x9d\x92\x8a\xf0\x9d\x92\x91\xf0\x9d\x92\x93\xf0\x9d\x92\x8a\xf0\x9d\x92\x82\xf0\x9d\x92\x8f\xf0\x9d\x92\x90 \xf0\x9d\x91\xac. \xf0\x9d\x91\xb4\xf0\x9d\x92\x82\xf0\x9d\x92\x93\xf0\x9d\x92\x95\xf0\x9d\x92\x8a\xf0\x9d\x92\x8f\xf0\x9d\x92\x86\xf0\x9d\x92\x9b \xf0\x9d\x91\xb0\xf0\x9d\x91\xb0\xf0\x9d\x91\xb0, \xf0\x9d\x91\xa8\xf0\x9d\x92\x84\xf0\x9d\x92\x95\xf0\x9d\x92\x8a\xf0\x9d\x92\x8f\xf0\x9d\x92\x88 \xf0\x9d\x91\xae\xf0\x9d\x92\x86\xf0\x9d\x92\x8f\xf0\x9d\x92\x86\xf0\x9d\x92\x93\xf0\x9d\x92\x82\xf0\x9d\x92\x8d \xf0\x9d\x91\xb4\xf0\x9d\x92\x82\xf0\x9d\x92\x8f\xf0\x9d\x92\x82\xf0\x9d\x92\x88\xf0\x9d\x92\x86\xf0\x9d\x92\x93\n\n#INEC\n#INECofficial\n#UnauthorizedConnection'

b'GMs REPORT\nJanuary 8, 2024\n\nOn January 6-7, 2024, some cell sites of Smart Communications were operating on generators  after power was disconnected for non payment of electric bills amounting to more than P2 Million in arrears.\n\nToday, January 8, 2024, representatives of Smart Communication settled their account with INEC Management resulting in the reconnection of power to these cell sites.\n\nThis is a much appreciated development on the Smart Communications account. It is of vital importance to INEC\xe2\x80\x99s renewed thrust in collecting all unpaid accounts and in improving it\xe2\x80\x99s collection efficiency. This is in line with measures towards the financial recovery  of INEC to ensure the viability of your  Electric Cooperative and provide more efficient and stable electrical power services to the Province of Ilocos Norte. \n\nDios Ti Agngina ti Agnanayon nga Suporta, Kailian! \n\xe2\x80\x93 \xf0\x9d\x90\x82\xf0\x9d\x90\x88\xf0\x9d\x90\x8f\xf0\x9d\x90\x91\xf0\x9d\x90\x88\xf0\x9d\x90\x80\xf0\x9d\x90\x8d\xf0\x9d\x90\x8e \xe2\x80\x9c\xf0\x9d\x90\x8f\xf0\x9d\x90\x84\xf0\x9d\x90\x91\xf0\x9d\x90\x91\xf0\x9d\x90\x98\xe2\x80\x9d \xf0\x9d\x90\x84. \xf0\x9d\x90\x8c\xf0\x9d\x90\x80\xf0\x9d\x90\x91\xf0\x9d\x90\x93\xf0\x9d\x90\x88\xf0\x9d\x90\x8d\xf0\x9d\x90\x84\xf0\x9d\x90\x99 \xf0\x9d\x90\x88\xf0\x9d\x90\x88\xf0\x9d\x90\x88, \xf0\x9d\x90\xbc\xf0\x9d\x91\x81\xf0\x9d\x90\xb8\xf0\x9d\x90\xb6 \xf0\x9d\x90\xb4\xf0\x9d\x91\x90\xf0\x9d\x91\xa1\xf0\x9d\x91\x96\xf0\x9d\x91\x9b\xf0\x9d\x91\x94 \xf0\x9d\x90\xba\xf0\x9d\x91\x92\xf0\x9d\x91\x9b\xf0\x9d\x91\x92\xf0\x9d\x91\x9f\xf0\x9d\x91\x8e\xf0\x9d\x91\x99 \xf0\x9d\x91\x80\xf0\x9d\x91\x8e\xf0\x9d\x91\x9b\xf0\x9d\x91\x8e\xf0\x9d\x91\x94\xf0\x9d\x91\x92\xf0\x9d\x91\x9f\n\n#INECofficial\n#INEC\n#GMsReport'

b'It has come to our attention certain news reports that erroneously interpreted statements of the AGM re timely payment of INEC electrical bills.  \n\nIt has been the long time policy and practice of INEC that Member-Consumer-Owners (MCOs) with at least 2 months unpaid electricity bills are subjected to disconnection on the third month or third billing period. Hence, the statement of the AGM that electricity connections are cut off on the third month. \n\nBe that as it may, the undersigned would like to apologize for any misunderstanding my statement may have caused. \n\nRest assured, the undersigned, as your Acting General Manager, is wasting no effort to ensure that the financial recovery of your cooperative continues. (INEC) in a letter dated December 7, 2023 sought the assistance of Laoag City Mayor, the Honorable Michael Marcos Keon regarding the unpaid electricity bills of the Laoag City General Hospital (LCGH). Today, December 14, 2023, upon the Mayor\xe2\x80\x99s directive, the Laoag City General Hospital Management sought and have indeed reached an agreement with the undersigned representing your Ilocos Norte Electric Cooperative, towards the settlement of the issue at hand. \n\nINEC Management and its Board of Directors would like to express our gratitude to the Honorable Mayor for his immediate and prompt action on the matter. \n\nThis much appreciated development on the LCGH account is of vital importance to INEC\xe2\x80\x99s renewed thrust in collecting all unpaid accounts and in improving our collection efficiency. In so doing, we hope to ensure the financial stability of INEC and enable your electric cooperative to provide more efficient and stable electrical power services to the Province of Ilocos Norte. b'UPDATE: ENERGIZED AS OF 05:42 PM\n\nAs of 3:45PM, INEC team is still on standby for power restoration at the landslide site along Sitio Banquero, Brgy. Pancian, Pagudpud.\n\nOur team is waiting for DPWH to finish its clearing operations and give its go signal for us to conduct the restoration works. b'For the safety and welfare of our MCOs and the province of Ilocos Norte as a whole, INEC management deemed it prudent to temporarily turn off the power lines in Brgys. Pasaleng and Pancian in the Municipality of Pagudpud and the whole Municipality of Adams due to the cutting of neutral line caused by the landsline along Sitio Banquero, Brgy. Pancian, Pagudpud. \n\nOur team is already patrolling the area for restoration. b'GM\'s REPORT\nNovember 17, 2023\n\nThe management have been receiving reports and complaints of busted transformers, damaged poles and inferior quality of line equipment which pose danger and safety concerns to member-consumer-owners (MCOs) and cause unnecessary interruption of power and electric services in the Province of Ilocos Norte. \n\nTo resolve such concerns and ensure the safety and security of our MCOs, effective January 1, 2024, the Engineering Services Department (ESD), and the Construction, Operations and Maintenance Department (COMD) are hereby mandated to only process for the approval of the Acting General Manager those projects which line materials, poles and equipment were SOLELY purchased and procured by INEC. \n\nAny project implemented to the contrary shall be deemed made without authority and all consequences of such shall be the sole responsibility of any concerned INEC personnel without prejudice to any disciplinary, administrative and legal sanctions the company may impose over concerned INEC personnel. -AGM Cipriano "Perry" E. Martinez, III\n\n#INEC\n#INECofficial\n#gmsreport'

b'Today, October 26, 2023, INEC Management visited the Agua Grande Mini Hydro Power Plant (MHPP) located at Brgy. Pancian, Pagudpud. \n\nThis is in line with the initiative of the INEC Management to increase and improve renewable energy power sources to further decrease the electricity rates in the Province of Ilocos Norte. \n\nFor operational efficiency of MHPP, Engr. Albert M. Marcos was reinstated back as OIC Area Manager of INEC Area 4 (Adams-Bangui-Burgos-Dumalneg-Pagudpud) and Engr. Derwin A. Jose was appointed as the new MHPP Plant Manager. \n\nIn addition, due to a report by an INEC employee regarding third persons planning to cut or remove INEC owned mahogany trees, INEC Management visited the INEC Pole Farm to verify the report. Upon inspection, indeed, several trees were labeled and numbered for cutting. \n\nThe pole farm is essential to the operations of INEC as this is where INEC source some of its wooden poles utilized for installation and maintenance of electric lines.\n\n INEC Management is closely coordinating with DENR and the PNP regarding these reports in order to secure INEC\xe2\x80\x99s right of control and ownership over these properties.  - \xf0\x9d\x91\xa8\xf0\x9d\x92\x84\xf0\x9d\x92\x95\xf0\x9d\x92\x8a\xf0\x9d\x92\x8f\xf0\x9d\x92\x88 \xf0\x9d\x91\xae\xf0\x9d\x92\x86\xf0\x9d\x92\x8f\xf0\x9d\x92\x86\xf0\x9d\x92\x93\xf0\x9d\x92\x82\xf0\x9d\x92\x8d \xf0\x9d\x91\xb4\xf0\x9d\x92\x82\xf0\x9d\x92\x8f\xf0\x9d\x92\x82\xf0\x9d\x92\x88\xf0\x9d\x92\x86\xf0\x9d\x92\x93 \xf0\x9d\x91\xaa\xf0\x9d\x92\x8a\xf0\x9d\x92\x91\xf0\x9d\x92\x93\xf0\x9d\x92\x8a\xf0\x9d\x92\x82\xf0\x9d\x92\x8f\xf0\x9d\x92\x90 \xf0\x9d\x91\xac. \xf0\x9d\x91\xb4\xf0\x9d\x92\x82\xf0\x9d\x92\x93\xf0\x9d\x92\x95\xf0\x9d\x92\x8a\xf0\x9d\x92\x8f\xf0\x9d\x92\x86\xf0\x9d\x92\x9b, \xf0\x9d\x91\xb0\xf0\x9d\x91\xb0\xf0\x9d\x91\xb0 \n\n#INEC\n #INECofficial\n#GMsreport'

Baligat, Baay, Bungon, Dariwdiw, Billoca, Quiling (Norte & Sur), Valdez, Ablan, Callaguip, Camandingan, Cangrunaan, Rayuray, Baoa (West & East) Palongpong, San Julian, Ricarte, Naguirangan, Capacuan, Sumader, Palongpong, Parangopong, Camguidan, San Mateo, San Pedro &  Nalupta.\n\nMUNICIPALITY OF PAOAY: Brgys. Bacsil, Cabaguan, Cabangaran, Callaguip, Cayubog, Dolores, Laoa, Masintoc, Nalasin, Oaig-Upay-Abulao, Pambaran, Paratong (except sitio galpac), Pannaratan(Pob), Salbang, San Agustin, San Blas (Pob.), San-Juan, San Pedro (except Sitio Agpuldag, Sitio Aroz), San Roque (Pob), Sangladan (Pob), Santa Rita (except Sitio Madanay), Veronica, Surgui, Pasil, Sungadan, Nanguyudan, Nagbacalan, Mumulaan, Suba except sitio Sungrot and Taknir. \n\nCITY OF LAOAG: Sitio 4 of Brgy. Balacad. \n\nUpon receipt of the report, INEC personnel immediately proceeded with line patrol in close coordination with the National Grid Corporation of the Philippines (NGCP). \n\nThe line patrol found no problem with the INEC lines. \n\nSubsequently, upon further inspection the joint INEC/NGCP team discovered that the source of the power interruption was the Protection Breaker on the Currimao - San Nicolas line which is owned by NGCP. Corrective works by NGCP in their circuit breaker eventually enabled the restoration of power in the areas affected at 7:36 AM this morning. \n\nINEC will continue to work as partners with NGCP. We at INEC and in behalf of our 150,000 member consumers however reiterate our appeal for NGCP to continue and even fast track their upgrading works in the Province of Ilocos Norte. \n\nWe ask once again our member consumers in the Province of Ilocos Norte to bear with us on this issue. Rest assured however, INEC backed by the strong and unwavering support of the Governor of the province, Matthew Marcos Manotoc and by the good Senator Imee Marcos, will continue to find ways to better serve the Province of Ilocos Norte on its electricity requirements.\n\n#INECofficial\n#INEC\n#ngcpemergencyinterruption"

b"\xf0\x9d\x90\x8d\xf0\x9d\x90\x84\xf0\x9d\x90\x80 \xf0\x9d\x90\x8d\xf0\x9d\x90\x84\xf0\x9d\x90\x96\xf0\x9d\x90\x92 \xf0\x9d\x90\x94\xf0\x9d\x90\x8f\xf0\x9d\x90\x83\xf0\x9d\x90\x80\xf0\x9d\x90\x93\xf0\x9d\x90\x84\n\xf0\x9d\x90\x8e\xf0\x9d\x90\x9c\xf0\x9d\x90\xad\xf0\x9d\x90\xa8\xf0\x9d\x90\x9b\xf0\x9d\x90\x9e\xf0\x9d\x90\xab \xf0\x9d\x9f\x90, \xf0\x9d\x9f\x90\xf0\x9d\x9f\x8e\xf0\x9d\x9f\x90\xf0\x9d\x9f\x91\n\nNEA and Cisco Philippines are partnering to develop a Digital Dashboard Command Center (DDCC) that will help map areas lacking electricity access. Electric cooperatives (ECs) will connect their digital dashboards to this center, aiding in identifying underserved households and areas.\n\nAs part of their Ugnayan 2030 program, Cisco will donate the dashboard system to NEA. Once integrated, it will allow remote monitoring of service interruptions and assist in quick decision-making. The project rolls out in phases, with Benguet Electric Cooperative as the pilot.\n\nCurrently, NEA aims to use Cisco's dashboard to achieve 100% electrification by the end of President Marcos' term in 2028. Presently, only 89% of Filipino households have access to power, and President Bongbong Marcos is committed to achieving universal electricity access by the end of his tenure.\n\n#INECofficial\n#INEC\n#NEAnews"

b'\xf0\x9d\x90\x88\xf0\x9d\x90\x8d\xf0\x9d\x90\x84\xf0\x9d\x90\x82 \xf0\x9d\x90\x8f\xf0\x9d\x90\x91\xf0\x9d\x90\x84\xf0\x9d\x90\x92\xf0\x9d\x90\x92 \xf0\x9d\x90\x91\xf0\x9d\x90\x84\xf0\x9d\x90\x8b\xf0\x9d\x90\x84\xf0\x9d\x90\x80\xf0\x9d\x90\x92\xf0\x9d\x90\x84\n\xf0\x9d\x90\x92\xf0\x9d\x90\x9e\xf0\x9d\x90\xa9\xf0\x9d\x90\xad\xf0\x9d\x90\x9e\xf0\x9d\x90\xa6\xf0\x9d\x90\x9b\xf0\x9d\x90\x9e\xf0\x9d\x90\xab \xf0\x9d\x9f\x8f\xf0\x9d\x9f\x96, \xf0\x9d\x9f\x90\xf0\x9d\x9f\x8e\xf0\x9d\x9f\x90\xf0\x9d\x9f\x91\n\nEarlier today, September 18, 2023, Ilocos Norte Electric Cooperative, Inc. (INEC) headed by AGM Cipriano \xe2\x80\x9cPerry\xe2\x80\x9d E. Martinez III had a dialogue with the National Grid Corporation of the Philippines (NGCP) Officials  headed by District head Arnel S. Ocampo to discuss and find solutions to the recurring power interruptions brought about by the conduct of maintenance works of NGCP lines in the Province of Ilocos Norte. \n\nNGCP explained to INEC that they have three kinds of maintenance works affecting our electric lines, namely: (1) Annual Preventive Maintenance; (2) Corrective Maintenance and (3) Maintenance Works for Improvement. \n\nFor 2023, NGCP has finished all of their scheduled annual preventive maintenance activities in the province but are set to implement a few more corrective and improvement works on their lines. On this, AGM Martinez  asked for NGCP to afford INEC atleast one month notice for INEC to duly inform its members-consumers-owners (MCOs) so they have enough time to make the necessary preparations for the scheduled power interruption. Further, as a matter of policy, INEC will no longer give its approval to any NGCP request that will cause for any given area in the province of Ilocos Norte to have NGCP caused power interruption for more than 6 hours at a given instance.\n\nIn line with these points of discussion and until such time that INEC is satisfactorily assured in resolving the issues raised, \xf0\x9d\x90\x9a \xf0\x9d\x90\xac\xf0\x9d\x90\x9c\xf0\x9d\x90\xa1\xf0\x9d\x90\x9e\xf0\x9d\x90\x9d\xf0\x9d\x90\xae\xf0\x9d\x90\xa5\xf0\x9d\x90\x9e\xf0\x9d\x90\x9d
